// german-protocol.txt
// This example is modeled as described in
// "Regular Model Checking without Transducers"

Initial {
    init: s0;

    s0 -> s1 F;       // excGran
    s1 -> s2 0;       // curCm
    s2 -> s2 I000FFF; // initial process state

    accepting: s2;
}

closedUnderTransitions;
